 <tr style='mso-yfti-irow:4'>
  <td width=317 valign=top style='width:237.8pt;padding:0in 5.4pt 0in 5.4pt'>
  <p class=MsoNormal style='margin-top:12.0pt;margin-right:0in;margin-bottom:
  12.0pt;margin-left:0in;line-height:150%'><span style='font-size:16.0pt;
  line-height:150%'><o:p>&nbsp;</o:p></span></p>
  </td>
  <td width=1464 colspan=5 valign=top style='width:1097.7pt;padding:0in 5.4pt 0in 5.4pt'>
  <p class=MsoNormal style='margin-top:12.0pt;margin-right:0in;margin-bottom:
  12.0pt;margin-left:0in;text-align:justify;line-height:150%'><span
  style='font-size:20.0pt;line-height:150%'>The project comes at a time when
  many south-east Asian countries are undergoing rapid industrial revolution
  and industrialisation processes. This results in increasing demand for
  energy, particularly electricity. Sourcing a cheap, safe and reliable
  electricity supply is central to further economic development.<o:p></o:p></span></p>
  <p class=MsoNormal style='margin-top:12.0pt;margin-right:0in;margin-bottom:
  12.0pt;margin-left:0in;text-align:justify;line-height:150%'><span
  style='font-size:20.0pt;line-height:150%'>Higher education institutions are expected
  to produce technical staff, engineers, experts and tutors which will able to
  design, maintain and further develop advanced technical solutions, as well as
  to train other staff resources like technicians and managers, who will be up
  to the job and ready to effectively and efficiently adopted and use modern
  power technologies.<o:p></o:p></span></p>
  <p class=MsoNormal style='margin-top:12.0pt;margin-right:0in;margin-bottom:
  12.0pt;margin-left:0in;text-align:justify;line-height:150%'><span
  style='font-size:20.0pt;line-height:150%'>Currently, the subjects which are
  central to help build modern power engineers are not available from the
  projects partner universities, and the content of current classes and the
  delivery mechanism does not meet students' expectations and challenges
  related to the transformation of the power sector.<o:p></o:p></span></p>
  <p class=MsoNormal style='margin-top:12.0pt;margin-right:0in;margin-bottom:
  12.0pt;margin-left:0in;text-align:justify;line-height:150%'><span
  style='font-size:20.0pt;line-height:150%'>The consortium of seven European
  and Asian partners has won total project funding of almost 1 million under
  the competitive <a href="https://eacea.ec.europa.eu/erasmus-plus_en"><span
  style='color:windowtext;text-decoration:none;text-underline:none'>Erasmus+</span></a>
  Key Action 2 call. The consortium will develop and deliver state-of-the art
  Smart Power Engineering subjects and programmes through partner universities
  using innovative teaching and learning platform.</span><span
  style='font-size:16.0pt;line-height:150%'><o:p></o:p></span></p>
  </td>
  <td width=317 valign=top style='width:237.95pt;padding:0in 5.4pt 0in 5.4pt'>
  <p class=MsoNormal style='margin-top:12.0pt;margin-right:0in;margin-bottom:
  12.0pt;margin-left:0in;line-height:150%'><span style='font-size:16.0pt;
  line-height:150%'><o:p>&nbsp;</o:p></span></p>

  <p class=MsoNormal style='margin-top:12.0pt;margin-right:0in;margin-bottom:
  12.0pt;margin-left:0in;text-align:justify;line-height:150%'><span
  style='font-size:20.0pt;line-height:150%;color:black;mso-color-alt:windowtext'>Atma
  Jaya Catholic University of Indonesia (Indonesia)</span><span
  style='font-size:20.0pt;line-height:150%'><o:p></o:p></span></p>
  </td>
 </tr>
 <tr style='mso-yfti-irow:9'>
  <td width=317 valign=top style='width:237.8pt;padding:0in 5.4pt 0in 5.4pt'>
  <p class=MsoNormal style='margin-top:12.0pt;margin-right:0in;margin-bottom:
  12.0pt;margin-left:0in;text-align:justify;line-height:150%'><span
  style='font-size:20.0pt;line-height:150%'><o:p>&nbsp;</o:p></span></p>
  </td>
  <td width=1464 colspan=5 valign=top style='width:1097.7pt;padding:0in 5.4pt 0in 5.4pt'>
  <p class=MsoNormal align=center style='margin-bottom:0in;margin-bottom:.0001pt;
  text-align:center;line-height:normal'><span style='font-size:20.0pt;
  mso-no-proof:yes'><!--[if gte vml 1]><v:shape id="Picture_x0020_4" o:spid="_x0000_i1034"
   type="#_x0000_t75" alt="wrld-21" style='width:1081.2pt;height:510pt;
   visibility:visible;mso-wrap-style:square'>
   <v:imagedata src="eACCESS_Uni_ver1_files/image007.jpg" o:title="wrld-21"/>
  </v:shape><![endif]--><![if !vml]><img border=0 width=1442 height=680
  src="eACCESS_Uni_ver1_files/image004.jpg" alt=wrld-21 v:shapes="Picture_x0020_4"><![endif]></span><span
  style='font-size:20.0pt'><o:p></o:p></span></p>
  </td>
  <td width=317 valign=top style='width:237.95pt;padding:0in 5.4pt 0in 5.4pt'>
  <p class=MsoNormal style='margin-top:12.0pt;margin-right:0in;margin-bottom:
  12.0pt;margin-left:0in;line-height:150%'><span style='font-size:16.0pt;
  line-height:150%'><o:p>&nbsp;</o:p></span></p>
  </td>
 </tr>
 <tr style='mso-yfti-irow:10'>
  <td width=317 valign=top style='width:237.8pt;background:#F2F2F2;mso-background-themecolor:
  background1;mso-background-themeshade:242;padding:0in 5.4pt 0in 5.4pt'>
  <p class=MsoNormal style='margin-top:12.0pt;margin-right:0in;margin-bottom:
  12.0pt;margin-left:0in;line-height:150%'><b style='mso-bidi-font-weight:normal'><span
  style='font-size:20.0pt;line-height:150%;color:black;mso-color-alt:windowtext'><a
  href="https://eaccess-edu.eu/"><span style='color:black;mso-color-alt:windowtext;
  text-decoration:none;text-underline:none'>Objective of the eACCESS project</span></a>:</span></b><b
  style='mso-bidi-font-weight:normal'><span style='font-size:20.0pt;line-height:
  150%'><o:p></o:p></span></b></p>
  <p class=MsoNormal style='margin-top:12.0pt;margin-right:0in;margin-bottom:
  12.0pt;margin-left:0in;line-height:150%'><span style='font-size:16.0pt;
  line-height:150%'><o:p>&nbsp;</o:p></span></p>
  </td>
  <td width=1464 colspan=5 valign=top style='width:1097.7pt;background:#F2F2F2;
  mso-background-themecolor:background1;mso-background-themeshade:242;
  padding:0in 5.4pt 0in 5.4pt'>
  <p class=MsoNormal style='margin-top:12.0pt;margin-right:0in;margin-bottom:
  12.0pt;margin-left:0in;text-align:justify;line-height:150%'><span
  style='font-size:20.0pt;line-height:150%;color:black;mso-color-alt:windowtext'><a
  href="https://eaccess-edu.eu/"><span style='color:black;mso-color-alt:windowtext;
  text-decoration:none;text-underline:none'>eACCESS project</span></a> will
  fill knowledge and skill deficit in the area of modern power system of the
  identified countries through knowledge dissemination, skill development and
  capacity building. These countries are facing challenges in supporting power
  and energy requirements due to lack of leadership, knowledge and facilities
  to develop skill personal in this region. eACCESS will mainly target <span
  class=GramE>this challenges</span> and offer required solutions through
  collaboration with local universities for enabling capacity building in
  Higher Education Sector.</span><span style='font-size:20.0pt;line-height:
  150%'><o:p></o:p></span></p>
  <p class=MsoNormal style='margin-top:12.0pt;margin-right:0in;margin-bottom:
  12.0pt;margin-left:0in;text-align:justify;line-height:150%'><span
  style='font-size:20.0pt;line-height:150%;color:black;mso-color-alt:windowtext'>The
  implementation of the <a href="https://eaccess-edu.eu/"><span
  style='color:black;mso-color-alt:windowtext;text-decoration:none;text-underline:
  none'>eACCESS project</span></a> will also benefit local energy companies,
  which will gain access to new, well-educated engineering staff, will be able
  to undertake research cooperation with local universities in the
  implementation of new solutions and the application of new technologies in
  power engineering.</span><span style='font-size:16.0pt;line-height:150%'><o:p></o:p></span></p>
  </td>
  <td width=317 valign=top style='width:237.95pt;background:#F2F2F2;mso-background-themecolor:
  background1;mso-background-themeshade:242;padding:0in 5.4pt 0in 5.4pt'>
  <p class=MsoNormal style='margin-top:12.0pt;margin-right:0in;margin-bottom:
  12.0pt;margin-left:0in;line-height:150%'><span style='font-size:16.0pt;
  line-height:150%'><o:p>&nbsp;</o:p></span></p>
  </td>
 </tr>
 <tr style='mso-yfti-irow:11'>
  <td width=317 valign=top style='width:237.8pt;padding:0in 5.4pt 0in 5.4pt'>
  <p class=MsoNormal style='margin-top:12.0pt;margin-right:0in;margin-bottom:
  12.0pt;margin-left:0in;text-align:justify;line-height:150%'><b
  style='mso-bidi-font-weight:normal'><span style='font-size:20.0pt;line-height:
  150%'>Specific role of Atma Jaya Catholic University <span class=GramE>Of</span>
  Indonesia (ATM):<o:p></o:p></span></b></p>
  </td>
  <td width=1464 colspan=5 valign=top style='width:1097.7pt;padding:0in 5.4pt 0in 5.4pt'>
  <p class=MsoNormal style='margin-top:12.0pt;margin-right:0in;margin-bottom:
  12.0pt;margin-left:0in;text-align:justify;line-height:150%'><span
  style='font-size:20.0pt;line-height:150%'>In the framework of this project,
  ATM will modernize the existing undergraduate curriculum in electrical
  engineering with new subjects dealing with smart power systems, smart grids,
  power economics.<o:p></o:p></span></p>
  <p class=MsoNormal style='margin-top:12.0pt;margin-right:0in;margin-bottom:
  12.0pt;margin-left:0in;text-align:justify;line-height:150%'><span
  style='font-size:20.0pt;line-height:150%'>Regarding the upgrade of the
  teaching facilities ATM will build Computer Simulation Laboratory (CSL) which
  will be shared also with SCU (<span class=SpellE>Soegijapranata</span>
  Catholic University).<o:p></o:p></span></p>
  <p class=MsoNormal style='margin-top:12.0pt;margin-right:0in;margin-bottom:
  12.0pt;margin-left:0in;text-align:justify;line-height:150%'><span
  style='font-size:20.0pt;line-height:150%'>Beyond that ATM will organize and
  conduct professional training program(s) for the local power industry. ATM
  will also introduce the <span class=SpellE>eACCESS</span> teaching platform
  for the delivery of the teaching material and will use it in the management
  of the teaching process. ATM will be mainly active in the work package WP2
  where it will lead the task T2.6, in the work package WP4 where it will lead
  the task T4.5, as well as in the work package WP6 coordinating the
  preparation of dissemination events<o:p></o:p></span></p>
  <p class=MsoNormal style='margin-top:12.0pt;margin-right:0in;margin-bottom:
  12.0pt;margin-left:0in;text-align:justify;line-height:150%'><span
  style='font-size:20.0pt;line-height:150%'>and dissemination materials (T6.3).<o:p></o:p></span></p>
  <p class=MsoNormal style='margin-top:12.0pt;margin-right:0in;margin-bottom:
  12.0pt;margin-left:0in;text-align:justify;line-height:150%'><span
  style='font-size:20.0pt;line-height:150%'>Details:<o:p></o:p></span></p>
  <p class=MsoListParagraphCxSpFirst style='margin-top:12.0pt;margin-right:
  0in;margin-bottom:12.0pt;margin-left:.5in;mso-add-space:auto;text-align:justify;
  text-indent:-.25in;line-height:150%;mso-list:l0 level1 lfo2'><![if !supportLists]><span
  style='font-size:20.0pt;line-height:150%;font-family:Symbol;mso-fareast-font-family:
  Symbol;mso-bidi-font-family:Symbol'><span style='mso-list:Ignore'><span
  style='font:7.0pt "Times New Roman"'>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp; </span></span></span><![endif]><span
  style='font-size:20.0pt;line-height:150%'>WP2: Development and/or
  modernization of the electrical power engineering curriculum, modernization
  and validation of teaching methods. (T2.6: Validation of the core teaching
  modules)<o:p></o:p></span></p>
  <p class=MsoListParagraphCxSpMiddle style='margin-top:12.0pt;margin-right:
  0in;margin-bottom:12.0pt;margin-left:.5in;mso-add-space:auto;text-align:justify;
  text-indent:-.25in;line-height:150%;mso-list:l0 level1 lfo2'><![if !supportLists]><span
  style='font-size:20.0pt;line-height:150%;font-family:Symbol;mso-fareast-font-family:
  Symbol;mso-bidi-font-family:Symbol'><span style='mso-list:Ignore'><span
  style='font:7.0pt "Times New Roman"'>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp; </span></span></span><![endif]><span
  style='font-size:20.0pt;line-height:150%'>WP4: Development and modernization
  of teaching facilities. (T4.5: Equipment acquisition and installation at <span
  class=SpellE>eACCESS</span>-CSL location. Set-up and commissioning of the
  physical laboratory)<o:p></o:p></span></p>
  <p class=MsoListParagraphCxSpLast style='margin-top:12.0pt;margin-right:0in;
  margin-bottom:12.0pt;margin-left:.5in;mso-add-space:auto;text-align:justify;
  text-indent:-.25in;line-height:150%;mso-list:l0 level1 lfo2'><![if !supportLists]><span
  style='font-size:20.0pt;line-height:150%;font-family:Symbol;mso-fareast-font-family:
  Symbol;mso-bidi-font-family:Symbol'><span style='mso-list:Ignore'><span
  style='font:7.0pt "Times New Roman"'>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp; </span></span></span><![endif]><span
  style='font-size:20.0pt;line-height:150%'>WP6: Dissemination and Exploitation
  of Project Results (T6.3: Production &amp; dissemination of project
  promotional materials)<o:p></o:p></span></p>
  </td>
  <td width=317 valign=top style='width:237.95pt;padding:0in 5.4pt 0in 5.4pt'>
  <p class=MsoNormal style='margin-top:12.0pt;margin-right:0in;margin-bottom:
  12.0pt;margin-left:0in;text-align:justify;line-height:150%'><span
  style='font-size:20.0pt;line-height:150%'><o:p>&nbsp;</o:p></span></p>
  </td>
